    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer11558458238356116747">Welcome to Clay Point, Louisiana, home to not-so-average Joes, and Nonie Broussard, a feisty Cajun and trouble magnet. After losing her job when the Garmin factory shuts down, Nonie is left with major money issues—as in, she has none. Desperate, she has to turn to the one place she’s avoided working since dropping out of college--her family’s funeral home.<br/>It wasn’t that No</span>
  <span id="freeText11558458238356116747" style="display:none">Welcome to Clay Point, Louisiana, home to not-so-average Joes, and Nonie Broussard, a feisty Cajun and trouble magnet. After losing her job when the Garmin factory shuts down, Nonie is left with major money issues—as in, she has none. Desperate, she has to turn to the one place she’s avoided working since dropping out of college--her family’s funeral home.<br />It wasn’t that Nonie feared the dead. In fact the opposite was true. She sees them—literally, and had been seeing the dead ever since she can remember. She tried telling her parents about it when she was a child, but they’d vehemently dismissed it to imaginary friends, so she’d stopped talking about it. There were only two people who actually knew Nonie’s secret and knew she was the real deal. One was Buggy Mouton, her best friend since kindergarten, and the other was Guy Skinard, whom Nonie considered her one true love since the day she’d laid eyes on him in high school. Buggy now worked at MeeMaw’s Café off of Main in Clay Point, and Guy, as usual, remained ever at her side—the only difference being he’d died in a freak boating accident nine years ago. Still the prankster even in death, Guy loved causing chaos, especially with men Nonie occasionally dated. She could only imagine what mayhem he might stir up while mirroring her at the funeral home and mingling with the newly departed.<br />Only hours into the first day of her new job, pandemonium engulfs the funeral home, and much to Nonie’s surprise, it has nothing to do with Guy. It’s brought on by the family they’re serving. Seventy-two–year-old Dover Fontenot, the Major of Clay Point, dies in a car accident after indulging in a little extra-curricular activity—only the activity wasn’t with his wife , Hazel. And when Dover’s mistress, Anna Mae Turner, shows up at the funeral home for the visitation hell’s gates rip open and Broussard’s Funeral Home suddenly turns into a geriatric war zone.<br />Amidst the flying hairpieces, canes and curses, Nonie’s best friend, Buggy, decides to drop by the funeral home with news she can’t wait to share. A cable network in New Orleans wants to put together a paranormal investigation team and have them check out purported haunted locations in Louisiana. For every location with solid filming potential, each member of the team gets a five hundred dollar pay check. And Buggy knows without question that if anyone can sniff out the ‘restless’ dead, it’s Nonie.<br />Knowing nothing about paranormal investigation, but lured by the sound of the adventure and the dollar signs circling through her head, Nonie agrees to become part of the Boo Krewe, the name Buggy has formally given the makeshift team.<br />The lure of money may be one thing, but what Nonie doesn’t realize is that occasionally the dead, so excited that someone can actually see and hear them, decide to follow her home, into her bed—the bathroom—the shower. And adding to this new-found frustration, Nonie barely finishes her first investigation when she gets a visit from Anna Mae Turner—the mayor’s former mistress—now dead, as well, and harassingly insistent that Nonie bring her killer to light.<br />Nonie quickly learns that the ‘gift’ she’s carried since birth is really a giant wart on the butt of life—and no amount of Compound W is going to make it go away!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11558458238356116747" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10534780327846013606">I loved this book! A great to start to a series and I cannot wait to read the others. Nonie Broussard and in fact all the characters were fantastic. I highly recommend. </span>

    <a title="Sparrow" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/116410597-sparrow"><img alt="Sparrow" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sparrow" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sparrow" href="/user/show/116410597-sparrow">Sparrow</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3375527352" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4735098755681081767">I really enjoyed this, and it seems like this is a new style for the author from looking at her other books. In my opinion she's written a fantastic book and it certainly suits her. I loved the spooky feel of the story and the humour interjected made it fun and so easy to read. In fact reading the whole thing in one weekend may be a record for me I loved it that much. I really hope to see more like this from Deborah Leblanc, I would certainly be buying it. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3350613086" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3350613086" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3350613086?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/40103806-toe-to-toe">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3350613086" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6063128563108729185">A strange and unusually entertaining dark story!<br/><br/>Louisiana author Deborah LeBlanc is not only an award-winning author: she is also a licensed death scene investigator and a paranormal investigator (also known as ghost hunter and occult investigator). In addition to her honors and positions of stature with the Horror Writers Association and the Mystery Writers of America, she is the founder of Literacy Inc, a non-profit organization to fight illiteracy and advocate motivation in America’s teenager</span>
  <span id="freeText6063128563108729185" style="display:none">A strange and unusually entertaining dark story!<br /><br />Louisiana author Deborah LeBlanc is not only an award-winning author: she is also a licensed death scene investigator and a paranormal investigator (also known as ghost hunter and occult investigator). In addition to her honors and positions of stature with the Horror Writers Association and the Mystery Writers of America, she is the founder of Literacy Inc, a non-profit organization to fight illiteracy and advocate motivation in America’s teenagers.<br /><br />With this novel Deborah LeBlanc opens a new series that has enormous promise – the Nonie Broussard Ghost Tracker Series. Though all of her novels are of the dark occult range, this series introduces a lead character in Nonie Broussard who is a medium, and for those unfamiliar with the term, a medium is one who communicates between the natural world and the spiritual world. This may be a tough assignment for other writers, but for Deborah, she inhabits the role, even is to serve as the ‘clairsendium’ for an upcoming paranormal investigation television series!<br /><br />Creating such a character requires skill, and in the very opening the book Deborah demonstrates her talent: ‘Panting, Nonie Broussard struggled to pull off Dover Fontenot’s underwear. The man weighed well over three hundred and fifty pounds and carried most of that lard in his barrel-chest, gut and butt. Fortunately, Nonie’s father had been gracious enough to cover Dover’s face with a sheet of black plastic so she didn’t have to look at it. In life, Dover had been no Brad Pitt. He’d looked more like a pit bull. A sixty-three-year-old, cigar smoking, bourbon-drinking foul-mouth pit bull and the mayor of Clay Point. LA…’ <br /><br />Using her fine-tuned skill at blending strange creatures and dark situations with fine wry humor, this story unfolds as follows: ‘Nonie Broussard is a medium—a closet medium. After losing her job at a local T-shirt factory, Nonie has to find a way to make ends meet. Not easy in a small town like Clay Point, LA. Two opportunities come her way, however, neither of them easy for someone with her abilities. Throw that medium into a funeral home and paranormal investigations with a gaggle of misfits, all because she has to pay the rent, and watch the fireworks fly!’<br /><br />This is one fine novel and a strong beginning of a most promising series. Hats off to a Pro! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6063128563108729185" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3401548231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4591651491384012131">Toe to Toe by Deborah LeBlanc is the funniest horror novel you will read. Nonie Broussard lives deep in Cajun country were mysterious events are common place. Her ability to see and speak to the dead is unique even for this place. She tries hiding her medium gift when her friend, Buggy, recruits her to work as a team of novice ghost hunters. She is reluctant, afraid her secret will get out. As much as she enjoys the handsome team leader, she fears discovery. Even worse is how ghosts come to her </span>
  <span id="freeText4591651491384012131" style="display:none">Toe to Toe by Deborah LeBlanc is the funniest horror novel you will read. Nonie Broussard lives deep in Cajun country were mysterious events are common place. Her ability to see and speak to the dead is unique even for this place. She tries hiding her medium gift when her friend, Buggy, recruits her to work as a team of novice ghost hunters. She is reluctant, afraid her secret will get out. As much as she enjoys the handsome team leader, she fears discovery. Even worse is how ghosts come to her to solve their problems.<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed Toe to Toe. Deborah LeBlanc is known for her skill and talent in horror novels, but this one has just the right twist to keep it light and humorous. The pace builds as Nonie is bombarded with drama from work, guys, and ghost hunting. I would love to see more books featuring Nonie the ghost tracker. <br /></span>

<div id="review_3482236916" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3482236916" />
    <a title="Grymm Gevierre" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/110261611-grymm-gevierre"><img alt="Grymm Gevierre" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582658997p2/110261611.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3482236916?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grymm Gevierre" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grymm Gevierre" href="/user/show/110261611-grymm-gevierre">Grymm Gevierre</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3482236916" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer140362830660386272">The Nonie Broussard series is one to keep an eye on!<br/><br/>This is my first time reading anything by Deborah LeBlanc, and I found that she is an interesting author—a professional in a field relative to her supernatural writing style. It is very clear this professional experience lends knowledge to her writing…at least particularly in this story. <br/><br/>Toe to Toe is the first story in the Nonie Broussard Ghost Tracker series. The story starts off immediately introducing us to Nonie as she is working her day j</span>
  <span id="freeText140362830660386272" style="display:none">The Nonie Broussard series is one to keep an eye on!<br /><br />This is my first time reading anything by Deborah LeBlanc, and I found that she is an interesting author—a professional in a field relative to her supernatural writing style. It is very clear this professional experience lends knowledge to her writing…at least particularly in this story. <br /><br />Toe to Toe is the first story in the Nonie Broussard Ghost Tracker series. The story starts off immediately introducing us to Nonie as she is working her day job for her family. LeBlanc masterfully paints the picture of Clay Point in the first few paragraphs of the book. Clay Point, LA isn’t real, but it feels like a real place. The characters are relatable and are in character for their region. I feel that Nonie is a fictionalized resemblance of LeBlanc, and I think that helps this character really pop. Eventually romance creeps it way it, and (insert eyeroll), it does get cliché at times…but LeBlanc never let it get overboard and ruin the main story. It was a solid b- plotline. <br /><br />This book stands out as a supernatural comedy, with horror undertones. This is a unique mix by itself, but coupled with the author’s skill and experience it really puts this series high on the watchlist. I could be biased as darker humor is my wheelhouse, but I really enjoy this read. This book really kicks everything off, really opening to a world that is interesting and well worth the read. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="140362830660386272" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2801039570161475168">TOE TO TOE is a Nonie Broussard Mystery, a Paranormal Cozy Mystery with a comfortable South Louisiana setting. Nonie, who contrary to personal preference works in the family funeral home, desires a "Normal" life, not one in which she sees or senses the dead. One of her best friends is her childhood sweetheart--who died tragically 9 years ago. Her other best friend persuades Nonie into a gig scouting ghosts for a New Orleans tv station! There goes normal.</span>

<div id="review_3506751898" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3506751898" />
    <a title="Gabby" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2931966-gabby"><img alt="Gabby" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3506751898?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gabby" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gabby" href="/user/show/2931966-gabby">Gabby</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3506751898&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3506751898" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4423729585637547792">Toe to Toe features Nonie Broussard, a young woman who has the dubious honor of being able to see and speak to dead people. When a paranormal TV show begins looking for scouting teams in the area, Nonie’s best friend volunteers her and a few other townsfolk she’s cobbled together into a ghost-scouting team. After a mayor’s wake goes sideways thanks to his wife and mistress fighting, the mistress ends up missing and the missing woman’s sister enlists Nonie’s assistance looking for clues when her </span>
  <span id="freeText4423729585637547792" style="display:none">Toe to Toe features Nonie Broussard, a young woman who has the dubious honor of being able to see and speak to dead people. When a paranormal TV show begins looking for scouting teams in the area, Nonie’s best friend volunteers her and a few other townsfolk she’s cobbled together into a ghost-scouting team. After a mayor’s wake goes sideways thanks to his wife and mistress fighting, the mistress ends up missing and the missing woman’s sister enlists Nonie’s assistance looking for clues when her home begins showing signs of poltergeist activity. Nonie, thanks to her abilities, sews the case shut quickly and the book feels truncated as several avenues for more exploration are suddenly cut off, making the book feel as though the author simply decided to stop for the day and slapped a “The End” on it and called it good. <br /><br />**SPOILERS**<br /><br />It was an entertaining enough book, but there was so much brought into the story that wasn’t expanded on. Why couldn’t Nonie see the mayor’s mistress’ ghost? Everything seemed to be handled pretty easily with the police investigation into the murder, so what exactly was Guy afraid of Nonie getting mixed up in? What happened to the ghosts from the places she and the Boo Krewe scouted? What about her dates? I get that the author wanted material to continue on into a series, but in my opinion she did too much setup and not enough follow-through in this book. That really killed a lot of the enjoyment for me. <br /><br />I received a free ARC in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4423729585637547792" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3629235764" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3629235764" />
    <a title="Luis Humberto Molinar Márquez" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56536968-luis-humberto-molinar-m-rquez"><img alt="Luis Humberto Molinar Márquez" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1467911475p2/56536968.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3629235764?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Luis Humberto Molinar Márquez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Luis Humberto Molinar Márquez" href="/user/show/56536968-luis-humberto-molinar-m-rquez">Luis Humberto Molinar Márquez</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56536968-luis-humberto-molinar-m-rquez?shelf=randr">randr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3629235764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6221428523155011377">[English review + Reseña en español]<br/><br/><i>Toe to Toe</i>, by Deborah LeBlanc <br/>LeBlanc Laboratories. 2018<br/>663 pages.	<br/>Fiction / Romance, mistery, ghosts<br/><br/>Nonie Broussard has started working at her family's funeral home in Clay Point, L.A. solely because she urgently needs a source of income. Meanwhile, a certain television station is in the area looking for an exploration team to visit some houses that have a reputation for being haunted, to record the pilot of their new television program, so Buggy, Nonie's fr</span>
  <span id="freeText6221428523155011377" style="display:none">[English review + Reseña en español]<br /><br /><i>Toe to Toe</i>, by Deborah LeBlanc <br />LeBlanc Laboratories. 2018<br />663 pages.	<br />Fiction / Romance, mistery, ghosts<br /><br />Nonie Broussard has started working at her family's funeral home in Clay Point, L.A. solely because she urgently needs a source of income. Meanwhile, a certain television station is in the area looking for an exploration team to visit some houses that have a reputation for being haunted, to record the pilot of their new television program, so Buggy, Nonie's friend, has seen a great opportunity in it for both of them to earn some extra income. Along with a team of strangers, Nonie must explore those places while she clarifies the direction that her heart will take, torn between the iron love of her ghost boyfriend and the new romances that knock on the door of her heart.<br />This book of supernatural romance and adventure, whose approach reminds me of the television series Ghost Whisperer, is part of the Nonie Broussard Ghost Tracker Series, by the same author. The plot centers on Nonie, a girl who lives with the spirit of her dead boyfriend while she tries to elucidate the path that her life will take now that he (or rather, his body) is no longer next to her. The plot is light and mixes several genres: supernatural mystery, crime and romance. Throughout the book a couple of mysteries are solved, although the book has left me with that peculiar sense of incompleteness typical of graphic novels published in installments and serial television programs.<br />Recommended for lovers of that area that mixes spooky supernatural mystery with romance, and of episodic stories. <br /><br />-------<br /><br /><i>Toe to Toe</i>, de Deborah LeBlanc.<br />LeBlanc Laboratories. 2018<br />663 páginas<br />Ficción / Romance, misterio, fantasmas<br /><br />Nonie Broussard ha comenzado a trabajar en la funeraria de su familia en Clay Point, L.A. únicamente porque necesita con urgencia una fuente de ingresos. Mientras tanto, cierta televisora está en la zona en busca de un equipo de exploración que visite algunas casas que tienen fama de embrujadas, para grabar el piloto de su nuevo programa televisivo, así que Buggy, amiga de Nonie, ha visto en ello una gran oportunidad de que ambas obtengan ingresos extras. Junto a un equipo de desconocidos, Nonie deberá explorar esos sitios mientras aclara el rumbo que tomará su corazón, dividido entre el férreo amor de su novio fantasma y los nuevos romances que tocan la puerta de su corazón.<br /><br />Este libro de romance y aventura sobrenatural, cuyo enfoque me recuerda a la serie de televisión Ghost Whisperer, es parte de la serie “Nonie Broussard Ghost Tracker Series”, de la misma autora. La trama se centra en Nonie, una chica que convive con el espíritu de su novio muerto mientras trata de dilucidar el camino que tomará su vida ahora que él (o mejor dicho, su cuerpo) ya no está a su lado. La trama es ligera y mezcla varios géneros: misterio sobrenatural, crimen y romance. A lo largo del libro se resuelven un par de misterios, aunque el libro me ha dejado con esa peculiar sensación de incompletitud típico de las novelas gráficas por fascículos o de los programas de televisión seriados.<br /><br />Recomendable para los amantes de esa zona que une el misterio sobrenatural fantasmagórico con el romance y las historias episódicas.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6221428523155011377" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

She can see and speak to the dead, including her boyfriend, who died in a boating accident 9 years ago. When a TV station starts looking for a group who can scout out haunted houses, Noni and her friends get the job. With Noni's skills (which she is trying to keep hidden) they are a shoo in to discover whether or not a place is haunted. Problem is, several ghosts follow her home with agenda</span>
  <span id="freeText4558733790037449033" style="display:none">A cute and original start to a series. Noni works at her dad's funeral parlor, with a special little perk. She can see and speak to the dead, including her boyfriend, who died in a boating accident 9 years ago. When a TV station starts looking for a group who can scout out haunted houses, Noni and her friends get the job. With Noni's skills (which she is trying to keep hidden) they are a shoo in to discover whether or not a place is haunted. Problem is, several ghosts follow her home with agendas of their own. And how can she move forward and have a life when her dead boyfriend is jealous of every guy she tries to date? </span>

<div id="review_3505493125" class="review notext" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3505493125" />
    <a title="Hipolito Foulks" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/115928693-hipolito-foulks"><img alt="Hipolito Foulks" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590589229p2/115928693.jpg" /></a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xBZD/+E3lHPV+qi7ua38HVjUS4r2HlKYytF2zNwYDQL+MCotWmldG3LRHNpOWPbCjousQjiT3P+RrzB9EVv/mA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('aprq64fO6BEDivrDcTNMSxIgE60cXvc7ki9mXoB6vbZQvIM5PJAheaShTqKGxkaUxH/0ZdLTeVzJUSDvTTlPLA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer4567783102560255393">Deborah LeBlanc is an award-winning, best-selling author and business owner from Lafayette, Louisiana. She is also a licensed death scene investigator, a licensed private investigator and has been a paranormal investigator for over twenty years.   <span id="freeText4567783102560255393" style="display:none">Deborah LeBlanc is an award-winning, best-selling author and business owner from Lafayette, Louisiana. She is also a licensed death scene investigator, a licensed private investigator and has been a paranormal investigator for over twenty years. Deborah is currently the house ‘clairsendium’ for the upcoming paranormal investigation television show, Through the Veil.<br /> <br />She served four years as president of the Horror Writers Association, eight years as president of the Writers' Guild of Acadiana, and two years as president of Mystery Writers of America's Southwest Chapter. In 2007, Deborah founded Literacy Inc. a non-profit organization dedicated to fighting illiteracy in America’s teens. <br />For more information, visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.deborahleblanc.com">www.deborahleblanc.com</a> and <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.literacyinc.com">www.literacyinc.com</a><br />To support Deborah please visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.patreon.com/deborahleblanc">https://www.patreon.com/deborahleblanc</a><br /><br /></span>
